     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">IMPAC</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Staff</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="legislation/index.html">Legislation</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="projects/index.html">Projects</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We develop UC's positions on legislative issues and provide analysis and research in support of policy initiatives.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p><span>Issues Management, Policy Analysis &amp; Coordination (IMPAC) is responsible for coordinating&nbsp; the development of the university's position for state and federal legislation, as well as responses to state and federal legislative, gubernatorial, and other official requests. IMPAC provides policy analysis and research to further initiatives consistent with UC's policy agenda.</span></p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Jenny Kao" src="_images/S7_jkao_075.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> <a href="staff/staff-pages/jenny-kao.html">Jenny Kao</a> </p> 
         <p>Executive Director</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/impac_org_chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';

      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <div class="imgContain"> 
      <div class="textHover"> 
       <h2 style="color: #a22f27">NOW ON iBOOKS &amp; KINDLE!</h2> 
       <p>The UC Riverside General Catalog (2013-2014) is now available through the Apple iBookstore and the Amazon Kindle store! eBook formats are available across a large variety of devices.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7"> 
      <h3 class="shadow" style="font-size: 1.2em;">UC RIVERSIDE'S EBOOK CATALOG!</h3> 
      <p> It does everything the printed catalog did-- and more! Enhanced searching. Bookmarking! Links to departments,programs, and services! Best of all, it's always with you for easy access. </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-11 last"> 
      <div id="mid-container"> 
       <div id="mid-right"> 
        <ul class="nav"> 
         <li class="nav-one"><a href="#kindle" class="current">Kindle <span class="sup">&reg;</span></a></li> 
         <li class="nav-two"><a href="#ipad">iBooks <span class="sup">&reg;</span></a></li> 
        </ul> 
        <div class="list-wrap"> 
         <div id="kindle"> 
          <img class="kindle" src="/Images/catalog/kindle.png" alt="" width="81" height="115" /> 
          <p>Get your eBook Catalog! The eBook version of the UCR General Catalog is available now through Amazon Kindle.</p> 
          <a href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00F9U2FH2"> <img class="download" src="/Images/catalog/download.png" alt="Download the Kindle version of the catalog." /></a> 
         </div> 
         <div id="ipad" class="hide"> 
          <img class="ipad" src="/Images/catalog/ipad.png" alt="" width="93" height="114" /> 
          <p>The Apple<span class="sup">&reg;</span> iBook version of the General Catalog is now available at the iBookstore. For both your iPhone and iPad!</p> 
          <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/university-california-riverside/id708729205?mt=11"> <img class="download" src="/Images/catalog/download.png" alt="Download the Apple version of the catalog." /></a> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <!-- END List Wrap --> 
       </div> 
       <!-- END Mid Right --> 
      </div> 
      <!-- END Mid Container --> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3 class="shadow" style="font-size: 1.6em; margin-top: 20px;">THE 2013-2014 UCR GENERAL CATALOG</h3> 
      <img src="/Images/catalog/cover.png" alt="" class="page-lead" style="float: left; padding-right: 10px;" /> 
      <p style="margin-top: 31px; padding-right: 10px;"> UC Riverside has also made a commitment to sustainability and improving the environments we might impact. It is in that spirit that we offer our annual catalog in ebook format -- thereby offering users enhanced accessibility and searchability while greatly reducing the amount of paper used. Download your <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/university-california-riverside/id708729205?mt=11">Apple iBook</a> or <a href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00F9U2FH2">Kindle eBook</a> version of the General Catalog today! </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last getRows" style="margin: 25px 0 38px 0;"> 
      <p> <strong>Please note:</strong> We are experiencing a technological problem with the <strong>&quot;PDF-Searchable&quot;</strong> version of the catalog. If you have Adobe Acrobat or a similar program, you may search the PDF version of the catalog in the interim. We hope to have this resolved soon and thank you for your patience. </p> 
      <div class="span-6"> 
       <h3 class="cheshirecat" style="margin-bottom: 18px;">PDF</h3> 
       <img src="/Images/catalog/catalog-pdf.png" alt="" class="page-lead" style="float: left; padding-right: 10px;" /> 
       <p> <span>Use this option to print your own version, or section, of the catalog!</span> <a href="/content/pdfs/catalog/UCRCatalog_13_14.pdf"> <img src="/Images/catalog/get.png" alt="Download a PDF version of the catalog." class="page-lead" /></a> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span-6"> 
       <h3 class="cheshirecat" style="margin-bottom: 18px;">PDF--SEARCHABLE</h3> 
       <img src="/Images/catalog/catalog-scribd.png" alt="" class="page-lead" style="float: left; padding-right: 10px;" /> 
       <p> <span>To search the catalog for certain keywords and phrases, use this option!</span><a href="http://www.scribd.com/doc/178439140/UCR-General-Catalog-2013-2014"> <img src="/Images/catalog/get.png" alt="Download a searchable PDF version of the catalog." class="page-lead" /></a> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span-6 last"> 
       <h3 class="cheshirecat" style="margin-bottom: 18px;">ARCHIVES</h3> 
       <img src="/Images/catalog/catalog-archive.png" alt="" class="page-lead" style="float: left; padding-right: 10px;" /> 
       <p> <span>To research previous versions of the catalog check our online archive</span> <a href="/registrar/archives/default.aspx"> <img src="/Images/catalog/get.png" alt="Download old catalogs that have been archived." class="page-lead" /></a> </p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last smallCase" style="margin-top: 25px;"> 
      <p class="noBorder" style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic; line-height: 1em;"><strong>PLEASE NOTE:</strong> </p> 
      <p class="noBorder" style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic; line-height: 1em;"><span class="bottom">Every effort has been made to ensure the accuracy of the information presented in the University of California, Riverside General Catalog. However, all courses, course descriptions, instructor designations, curricular degree requirements, and fees described herein are subject to change or elimination without notice. Students should consult the appropriate department, school, college, or graduate division for current information, as well as for any special rules or requirements imposed by the department, school, college, or graduate division.</span></p> 
      <p class="noBorder" style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic; line-height: 1em;"><span class="bottom">The departmental websites referenced in this catalog are maintained by independent operators and do not necessarily reflect approved curricular and course information.</span></p> 
      <p class="noBorder" style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic; line-height: 1em;"><span class="bottom"><b>Accessibility:</b> The University of California, Riverside is committed to providing our documents in a manner that is accessible to all. If you need to view the catalog using a screen reader or other assistive software<a href="http://registrar.ucr.edu/content/pdfs/catalog/UCRCatalog_13_14.pdf" target="_blank"> please download the PDF version of the catalog</a>.</span></p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
